1b1(rgyud): de ba'i gshes pa zad kyi de 'o na rid smras pa zhes bya na
1b2(rgyud): rgya gar skad du/ sarba ta thA g+ha/ na ma mai hI yAn sutra/ bod skad du/ sangs rgyas
1b3(rgyud): dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// dpal rdo rje sems dpa'al phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis tho
1b4(rgyud): pa'i dus gcig na bcom ldan 'das dpal rnam par snang mdzad/ thugs rje chen de de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
2a1(rgyud): cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes// rnal 'byor chen po'i dbang phyug/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi phyag rgya thams cad mnyam pa nyid thugasu chud
2a2(rgyud): thangs cad kyi dgas pa snang bas/ mas can gyi 'ams mdzes shing rdzus pa med pa thams cad kyi thathams cad stos zhing ba'i 'dren lus mdzad pa/ 
2a3(rgyud): dus gsum sa rtag par 'bugs shing // sku dang gsung dang thugs thams cad rdo rjeg zur gyu pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa lam
2a4(rgyud): cad bzhugs shing bsngags pa// stong pa nur bu dang rin po che chen pos smra sa pa// kha dog sna tshogs pa'i dril bu btags pa/ dar dang 'phan dang / 
2a5(rgyud): me tog gi 'breng ba dang / rnga ma dra ba dang / dra ba byed pa dang / zla ba rlung gis skyod pa rnams kyis mdzes par byas pa// 'og min gyi lha'i rgyal po'i
2a6(rgyud): nas na// byang chub sems dpur b+he ra khrag dag zas dpa la 'dis ste// drung chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po brAbyA na rdo rje dang // kun tu spyan ras
2a7(rgyud): gshegs kyi dbang da// nas 'i snying po dang / na rgyang dang / seMs rnye pa zab tu rjes 'khor lo 'drer ba dang / ram mkha'i mad+hA dang / kyi sa
2a8(rgyud): rab tu 'joms pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po bye ba khrag dgu bcu rtsa dbu dang // gang gi 'akrung gi bye ma snyed kyi de bzhin/ 
2b1(rgyud): gshegs pa rnams dang / thabs gcig tu bzhugs te/ de yang 'di ltar 'dzam bu'i gling na/ de bzhin gshegs pa chang med grangs med pa de dag gi skus til gi gang bu/ 
2b2(rgyud): du.Ats+tsha ma pad+ma snang ngo // de nin gshegs pa'i sgra las kyang las rgyas kyi zhi bar med zas med pa rnams drang // sas rgyas kyi shing nga
2b3(rgyud): na yang chos kyi tshul 'di nyid 'chad do// de nas bcom ldan 'das rnams par snang mdzad chen po/ nam mkha'i dbyings bzhin du// thams cad na rtag par bzhugs shing
2b4(rgyud): sku dang // gsung dang thugs rdo rje lta zur gyur pa// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad drang mnyam pa nyid du 'jug pas rdo rje'i dbyings thams cad thugs su chud pa'i
2b5(rgyud): ye shes sems dpa'// nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad kyi rdul shin du phra mo'i rdo rje'i byin gyis rlabs las byung ba'i ye shes kyi snying po// de bzhin gshegs pa
2b6(rgyud): thams cad mnyes par byed ba'i phyir// rdo rje rin po che'i ye shes kyi dbang phyug rin po cher 'gyur ba/ rnag pa'i dbyis thams cad du rnas par mdzad pa'i
2b7(rgyud): bzhin nyid kyi ye shes mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pas// mngon par rdzogs par byang chub par 'gyur cing // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ngo bo nyid dag pa'i phyir// 
2b8(rgyud): chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin dag par thugs su chud pa// nam mkha'i khams thams cad du khyab pa'i gzugs thams cad du yang dag par snyan pa mkhyen pas// 
3a1(rgyud): sems can ma khas sum thas shing lus bskyed pa nasaspyod pa gon tu rgyas // de bzhin pashegs pa rnams cad du m-i ga bar du gcod pa med/ 
3a2(rgyud): pas/ thams cad dang mnyam pa med pas bla na med pa'i 'phrin la sa thams cad mdzod pa// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byang chub chen por sems dpa' brtan pa
3a3(rgyud): dang nga de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad spyan drang ba'i dam tshig dang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyes par bya ba'i ye shes kyi dbang phyug dang // de bzhin
3a4(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi legs so zhes bya ba dang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rin po che'i dbang bskur ba dang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
3a5(rgyud): nyi ma'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor dang // de bzhin gshegs thams cad kyi yid bzhi gyi nor bu'i rgyal po che'i dpal dang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
3a6(rgyud): bzhad pa chen po dang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi drag pa'i chos chen dang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi shes rab chen po'i ye shes dang / 
3a7(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor lo dang // de bzhin gshes pa thams cad kyi dgongs pa 'chang pa dang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gdon mi za bar thams cad
3a8(rgyud): gyi dgos pa mdzad pa dang // de bzhin gshes pa thams cad kyi brtson 'grus chen pa'i go cha shin tu dbang po dang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi srung zhing skyong ba'i gnod sbyin dang / 
3b1(rgyud): pa shegs pa mas pa myen sa rlung dang thags de rje byag rgya bangs pa'i leshes nasas kau// na yang da na / ra ma
3b2(rgyud): blo dang // mkha' skyes shin du gzi chen dang // rin chen dpal dang rdo rje 'dzum/ kun tu gzigs dang dbang rten dang // 'jam dpal dkyil 'khor thams cad dang / 
3b3(rgyud): mi gsung ba dang thams cad las// brtson 'grus ma rungs dpe du gzung / rdo rje lcags kyi mnga' 'gyu dang // rin rten nyi ma rnal mtshan 'dzum// pad mA rab dri 'khor lo gsung
3b4(rgyud): rdzas dang po rtsa 'jigs byed sangs// thog ma pa mi med cing ni// ma rungs 'gro la 'tshongab che// gnod sbyin srin po dam pa stan// ga'i can dpe'i dbang po
3b5(rgyud): u ma'i bdag po skye dbu'i 'tshon/ gtogs 'dod rgyal 'dod drul ba che// 'jig rten dang mkhams pa// 'jig rten skyong dang 'ams bsum pa// 'byung chen sem
3b6(rgyud): ngo rung lang / gas 'ad thamasas pa da// 'khod dang byung ngan 'das dang ga/ sang drug brgya dang me ba'i ma / sangs rgyas dag pa reg te// sred pasam nyam pa
3b7(rgyud): de yin no// 'jig rten gsum nub de spyod dang // bde skyong mngon po 'i rang tshul mdang // rdo rjeg tso rangs rab 'chog/ ye shes pha rol phyin pa'i chug/ byang chub
3b8(rgyud): dpa' rnam par thar// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi spyod// sangs rgyas don dong sangs thugs// byang chub kun dang bla med// rnam par snang 'dzang rgyal ba gtsud
4a1(rgyud): rang 'byung gzungs dang dran pa dang // sems dpa' che dang phrag rgya che/ ting 'dzin sangs rgyas 'phrin las 'dzad// yang dag sangs rgyas kun bdag nyid// yod pa rtag don rtogs
4a2(rgyud): mdzad pa// sdong chen chen po nag po che// 'dod chags chen po bde ba che// thabs chen dang ni mchog chen mchog/ kun gyi mchog dang gnas dbang po// bcom ldan 'das byang chub
4a3(rgyud): sgren po'i drugs/ d+hang chub sems dpa chen po kun tu yang ba'i// de 'di tu shegs pa thos cang kyi thugs pa da so// de nas de ba'i min shegs pa thams ca kyim pas rgyas
4a4(rgyud): kyi zhing 'di ni dper na til gyi gang bu bzhin du yongs srung bar gyur to// de nas dri bzhi gshegs pa thams cad 'dus te byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po don thams cad
4a5(rgyud): grub pa byang chub kyi snying por bzhugs pa gang na ba deng gshegs te// byang chub sems/ nyedapa' de la ched du longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku stan nas// 'di skad ces pas
4a6(rgyud): sprul to// rigs kyi bu khyod kyis gang gi phyir de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi de khon mngon par ma rtogs par// dga' bar snang bya thams cad la sto skyed cig/ 
4a7(rgyud): Ni wAr d+ha na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs pa cu bya snyam// de nas byang chub sems dpal sems dpa' chen po don/ thams cad zlu ba/ 
4a8(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis spel bas mi yo ba'i ting 'dzin de las bzhengs s+ho// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad phyag byas nas 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan
4b1(rgyud): 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnams/ de kho nyid ni ci lta bu lags// ci ltar ni sgrub par gyi bka' stsal du gsol// de skad ces gsol pa dang // de bzhin gshegs pa de ga thams cad
4b2(rgyud): kyis gsung gcig tu 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu rang gi sems la rtog cing mnyam par gzhog la rang bzhin gyis grub pa'i sngags 'dre ci dgar 'bras shing sgrub par gyis
4b3(rgyud): shig/ A~Mn+di tA pra ti be d+hang ka ro mi// de nas byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnams
4b4(rgyud): bdag gi snying len bzla ba'i dkyil 'khor lte bur bdar bar bdag gis rtogs so// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bka' stsal pa// rigs kyi kyi bu sems 'di ni rang bzhin
4b5(rgyud): gyis 'odo gsal bas na// de ni ci lta bur spungs pa de lta bur gyur te// deper na ris dkar po mtshon gyis smra bar bzhin no// de nas de bzhin gshen pa
4b6(rgyud): thams cad kyis rang bzhin gyi 'ong gas su kha'i sems shes pa rgyas bur bya ba'i phyir/ A~M.AM b+h+yo d+hi tsing ta ud sA ta sa mi// zhes rang bzhin gis thub pa'i sngags 'dis yang byung
4b7(rgyud): chub sems dpa' chen po de byang chub kyi sems skyed par gyur to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen pos yang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bkas byang chub kyi sems skyed
4b8(rgyud): nas 'di skad ces gsol to// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor lta bur mthong ba gang lags pa de ni zla ba'i dkyil 'khor nyid du mthong ngo // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bka' stsal pa// 
5a1(rgyud): de bzhi gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po sems skyed pa ban tu po stong kyis mngon las su du thar gyis de legs par sgrubs shig// de bzhin gags
5a2(rgyud): pa rnams cad kyis sems sted pa ban d+ha yang ba de nA ba rtsa bya mas dis 'ang di slong b+hA 'i dkyil 'khor la 'i rgyas sems shig tis dang / 
5a3(rgyud): byang chub sems dpas gsol ba// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs de rnams rna ba'i la 'khor che steng na// rdo rje bdag gis mthong do// de bzhin gshegs pa thangs
5a4(rgyud): zang kyis pa thub pa// de bzhin pashegs pa thams cad can tu yang bdi sems rje sngas sa na par byas sheg pa mAM 'jas rnam na nA~M// de nas nam 'brur / 
5a5(rgyud): thams cadan du mngam par 'jug pa de bzhin gshegs pa 'o/ cad kyi sku rang bsung kyi dang thug sa rdo rje dbyangs kyi stong pa de dag thams cad de bzhin gshes
5a6(rgyud): bya thams cad kyi byin gyig rnangs / sems dpardo rje de 'a bragaso// de bzhin ga shegs pa thams cad kyis/ bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa
5a7(rgyud): na pa den thams cad grub pa de 'ang dri rje dbyings shes rdo rje zhes bya ban+de bang sgyur ro// denas byang chub sems dpanga' rdo rje dkyis kyis de sazhidu gshegs pa de dag rnams cad la ni snang
5a8(rgyud): te// sa ma ldan 'das de zhi gagags pa rnams de 'dzid dgas pa mas / las lan ma / du da 'im pa yi kyi pa / 
5b1(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de lta bas na sems dang rdo rje rnam pa'i mcho ga thams cad dang dran pa'i sas rgyas kyi thur 'dab nyid rang bden pas grub pa'i sngags 'di ci dgang thos la som
5b2(rgyud): shig// oM ya thA sarba tra thA ga ta sa ya dza a haM// de nas de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i dbyis kyis bdag nyid de bzhin gshegs par mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas
5b3(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la phyag byas te// 'dri skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bdag byin gyis rlob sA lon/ mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa 'di rnan pa
5b4(rgyud): mdzod cig/ de skad ces gsol pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje'i dbyis kyis sems dpa'i rdo rje der thug so de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rjerje
5b5(rgyud): dbyis kyis mang ci ma do chen// de bzhin gshegs pa mis cad kyi mam pa nyid kyi shes mngon dar rdzogs par sangs rtsom gde bzhin gshegs pa thams cad pa rje
5b6(rgyud): mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes kyi drug rgyu bad+ma ba dam tshig tu gagade bzhin gshes la thams cad kyi rdo dzi rin pa che'i da pa sa gcad kyi phyag rgya bsang ba'i dang tshig tu zhugs// de 'di
5b7(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi chos mnyam nyid kyi ye shes rtogs pas rang bzhin gis ngag go// de bzhin dashegs pa thams cad kyi thams cad mnyam pa nyid rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal pa'i ye shes 'byung gan su gyur pa'i/ 
5b8(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyasu gyur to// de nas yang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sems dpa'i rdo rje de las de bzhin gshoT pa thams cad byung nas// de bzhin
6a1(rgyud): de bzhi gshegs pa payas cad dkyims panyid gyimi shes rnyed/ ba byung ba nod dran pa chen po nga byung na tu spyan rab rnaMs kyi nga cos kyis sa byed
6a2(rgyud): de na gshes pa thams cad kyi 'dzin las thams ca la banag nus// de rab mi ci ra d+h+wi gAs dang // / nga du rtse ba brje mo rdo rje dang // nor du ng+ge ba chims rgyas pa gangan pa der bas
6a3(rgyud): te byon nas// de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje'i dbyings de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad du byin gyis badrangs te// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi seng ge'i 'ang la zhal kun tu bstan te/ 
6a4(rgyud): banag par gyur to// bye bzhin gshegs pa mi spyod pa dang // de bzhin gshegs pa rin chen 'drang ba dang // de bzhin gshegs pa snyun ras gzigs kyi dbang ba'i rtul po dang // de bzhin g.yen
6a5(rgyud): pa mdon mi za bar grub pa rnams// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad rdum stonas das/ nyid byin gyis rnams te/ bcom ldan 'das rab rgya rdus de bzhin gshegs pas thams
6a6(rgyud): cad mnyam pa nyid du rab tu rtogs pa'i phyir// phyogs thams cad mnyam pa 'di du hU~M gas nas/ phyogs bzhir bzhug so// de nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang 'dzang
6a7(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa mngon par rdzorje par sangs rgyas nas ring po ma lon pa// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs kun tu bzang po zhes bya ba de bzhin gshes pa thams cad kyi mamakha
6a8(rgyud): las byung ba'i nor du rin po che chen po'i dbang gis dbang skur ba// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi kun tu spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i chos kyi ye shes dam pa'i pha rol tu phyin/ 
6b1(rgyud): ba brnyes pa de bzhin gshes pa thams cad kyi 'phrin las gdon mi za ba thams cad ston pa// thogs pa med pa'i dgongs pa rdzogs pa// yid kyi bsam pa 'od
6b2(rgyud): mchog yong su rdzogs pas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad du bdag cing bdag nyid kyis byin gyis rlabs nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byang chub kyi sems kun tu bzang po
6b3(rgyud): zhes bya ba'i dam tshig byung ba// sems dpa' byin gyis rlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyom par bzhugs nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thegs pa chen po mngon par rtogs
6b4(rgyud): pad+ma zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po 'di rang gis thugs ka nas byung ngo // badz+ra sad tra/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs ka nas byang ma zag pa 'di ni/ 
6b5(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das kun tu bzang po de nyid de zla ba'i dkyil 'khor du byung nas gyur nas byung ste// / sems can thams cad kyi byang chub kyi sems chen po yang dag par spangs nas/ 
6b6(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi phyogs phyog su 'khod do// de nas zla ba'i dkyil 'khor de dag las kyang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes kyi rdo rje drung ste/ 
6b7(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs su zhugaso rdo rje ses dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni shin du rtun pa dang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byin gyis rlabs
6b8(rgyud): kyis gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas/ nam mkha'i khams thams cad du 'ong bar rtse lnga pa'i 'phred pas khyab par bzhugs te/ dade bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang
7a1(rgyud): thugs ra la du 'i sa su byung bab// de bdu gshenas du rnams kyi tshugs nas rung ste// b+ha sa panas// de nas dzo wA bu'i 'od zer 'azugs dang // 'as
7a2(rgyud): rdzoms pa dang / 'jig rten po mas thams cad du snang ras chub par byed pa rnams rlung dus 'dzi rjes sun 'ang ze nga dag gi rtse mo pas 'a zhe pa mas thams cad kyi rnas
7a3(rgyud): zhing kyi na na rgyam du/ nga pa sa sem sus sa nga ji na
7a4(rgyud): sems rjedan de rnyed da/ lan du yang rlu sas sasu sa rjid kyi rinas mdzes pa mang ba dang // byang chub pa
7a5(rgyud): bo chen por gshegs pa dang // 'drang thams cad 'dul ba dang // de bzhin gshen pa thams cad kyi mnyam banyid kyi byang chub chen po mngon par byang chub pa dang // das pa
7a6(rgyud): chos kyi la lo banon pa nas sems can gyi/ mas ma thus shing zas pa zed ba rnanas yongs tshur ci/ thams cad la ban pa dang bde bang mang bdu/ de bzhin gshems
7b1(rgyud): rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi kun tu bzang po yin pa dang shin du rten pa yin pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas// byang chub sems dpa' chen po kun bzang po'i skur gyur te// bcom
7b2(rgyud): ldan ras rnam par snang 'dang ci thugs la gas nas// 'di snyed du ched du rjong pazod du bad // e ma he bdag ni rang 'byung bani/ kun tu 'alung ba sems dpa rtan// de ni na
7b3(rgyud): phyir lus min yang // sems dpa'i lus su gyur pa yin// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po'i sku bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs ka nas byung ste// de bzhin gshegs pa thams
7b4(rgyud): cad kyi spyan snga nas/ zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas bka' nod cing bzhugs par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes kyi dam tshig rdo rje zhes bya
7b5(rgyud): ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyom par bzhugs nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi tshul khrims dang // ting 'dzin dang / shes rab dang // rnam par grol ba dang / rnam par gro
7b6(rgyud): nga'i ye shes mthong ba dang // chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba dang sos can gyi don bya ba dang // thabs chen po dang de stobs chen po dang // brtson 'grus dang ye shes chen po'i dam tshig sems can gyi khams
7b7(rgyud): ma lus shing lus pa med pa'i rnams yongasu sgrub pa dang // thams cad kyi dbang por bya ba dang // thams cad bde ba dang // yid bde ba dang // myong bar bya nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mnyam/ 
7b8(rgyud): pa nyid kyi ye shes dang mngon par shes pa bla na med pa dang / theg pa chen po che mngon par rtogs pa mngon par grub pa'i mngon chog thob pa'i bar du 'bras bu de dag gi phyir// byang chub sems dpa' chen po kun
8a1(rgyud): tu bzang po de de bzhin gshegs pa thams kyi 'khor por sbyar ba nyid du sangs rgyas thams ca sku rin po che'i dgra rgyan dang gcod pan gyi dbang gis dbang sbyar nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams/ 
8a2(rgyud): cang kyi grub pa rdo rje de de'i lag par byin no// de bzhin dgags pa thams cad kyi lag na rdo rje lag na rdo rje zhes bya ba nga gis dbang du'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sos rapa
8a3(rgyud): chen pa lagan d+hi phyag g.yon pa rje rnyings par bsus// phyag gsas pas sa pa dpar zhi / smin pa'i rnal du 'an da// ded du rjong ba rdo da do// rang
8a4(rgyud): ri nan med // 'du// de rje ni na su sengs kyi yang byang chu rims pa 'a mapa
8a5(rgyud): dam mig drang ba'i sengs dpang byi nungs rdo yin la sems pang zhugs nas// de du na na gshegs pa thams cad spyan drang ba'i ngas kyis ces bya/ 
8a6(rgyud): ba de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po 'di rang gi thugs pa nas byung / badz+rad do// de nas de ni gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs ga nas byung ma thag pa
8a7(rgyud): ma ldan 'das tragan rje de gas ge nas stong das nga nga rung kyi su nas te ma tu ma
8a8(rgyud): ri mas byed pa kyi nadenas kyis bo sa/ 'a na gyi mam sa
8b1(rgyud): kyi rdul shingan du phra mo dang mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i sgra rnams byung ste// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad spyan drang ba la sogs pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul dang / cho 'phrul rnams
8b2(rgyud): sa nas rje sems dang me nge badzinani// tu 'a mim po'i khyim gyi yin pa dang / na pa'i phyim pa tu ches par gyur te// nang chub stongs dpang ched pa shi du 'du
8b3(rgyud): nga'i lus su gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das rna bar snang 'dzad kyi thugs la gnas te// cheng du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// oM mA rdo rje las byung ba'i// lcags kyu nges pa'i rgyal po dang / 
8b4(rgyud): gang phyir kun tu sangs rgyas khyadab// grub phyir kun nas spyan 'dren no// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po shin du gdon mi za ba'i rgyal po'i sku// bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs
8b5(rgyud): ka nas byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyigo/ yus phyogs kyi zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas bka' nod cing bzhugs par gyur to// de nas
8b6(rgyud): ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad spyan drang ba'i dam tshig gi rdo rje zhes kyo ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyems par zhugs nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad spyan drang ba'i
8b7(rgyud): tshig/ sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa thams cad dgug pa dang // thams cad kyi bde ba dang / yid byeng ba myong bar byas pa nas/ de bzhin gshes
8b8(rgyud): pa thams cad 'du ba'i byin rlabs dam pa'i bar du sgrub pa'i phyir/ rdo rje lcags kyu de byang chub sems dpa' gdon mi za pa'i rgyal po de'i log par de bzhin du byin na// 
9a1(rgyud): de zhin shegs pa yas da ci rje sags nas ra/ sa da DU nas dang su ston pa de rje zugs rgyu smra des
9a2(rgyud): nu sma nga dang sa nga sa skye ba che rlung ba kyai smras ji rje zhes bya ba'i di la sum na
9a3(rgyud): bar gas nas// de zhin gshegs pa rnams pa dgis pa byed mi rje na na gshegs pa 'angs kyi snying bu 'dzi nga gi zu ka u d+hA // badz+ran du
9a4(rgyud): sa das sa bya dis nga / sa sa kyi sa son te mas rgyas de'i rjem na du chung byed pa
9b1(rgyud): rab tu brtan pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas// byang chub sems dpa' chen po 'dud ces bya bar gyur te// bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang 'dzad kyi thugs la gnas
9b2(rgyud): nas// rjed du rjod pa 'di ched du rjod do// e ma bdag gi rang bzhin dag/ rang 'byung ba dag dgos byed de// 'dod 'chags bral rnams dag pa'i phyir// 'dod chags kyi ni
9b3(rgyud): yul bar byed// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po bdud de'i lus/ bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs nas rlung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad gson rlon su kyi
9b4(rgyud): zla da dkyil 'khor la gnas nas yang ka nad cing bzhu'o// de nas bcom ldan 'dusu de bzhin gshegs pa mnyes par bye dwa'i byin gis rlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting
9b5(rgyud): 'dzin pa snyoms par bzhugs nus// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi da rdo rje'i ngas khrims can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa rnams su bya ba dang / 
9b6(rgyud): rdzas cad kyi ze ba dang / yid med pa myong byur b+h+yasmra nas// de bzhin pa sheg sa ba thams cad kyi bdud kyi mchog 'grub pa thob pa'i bad+ma du 'azlas pa de dag gi phyir
9b7(rgyud): rdo rje rje byang chub seMs dang chen po 'dud ces bya ba'i phyag du de bzhin du byin no// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rnams cad kyis rdo rje gzung zhes d+hA rmu
9b8(rgyud): ba'i dbang gis dbang skur// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i bcu zhes bya bas rdo rje'i mnga' des// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la 'dud pa khyed cing // 
10a1(rgyud): ched du rjod pa 'di ched du rjod do// sangs rgyas kun gyi 'dod chags kyi/ ye shes 'di ni dri ma med// 'dod chags kyis ni chags bral bcom// bde ba thams cad sbyin par bye/ 
10a2(rgyud): denas ldan las kyis rang byang chub sems dpa' chen po rab tu dbar nga'i rgyal po'i dab ci zung ba/ smos dang byi byis rabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ti de dzin la sgoms par thums nas/ 
10a3(rgyud): de bzhi gshes pa thangasas kyi rang tu bya 'i dam kyi rjes rgyu 'di med rdzun gyi zhing pa rang 'i thugs gnas byu / rangs d+ha de nyid pan sa
10a4(rgyud): thams cad kyi thugs las byang ma thag tu 'di ni bcom ldan 'das rje rje 'dzin pa de rnyed/ med po zhes bya bar gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang 'ja
10a5(rgyud): kyi thugasu zhugasate te// gcig tu 'dres paragyur nasaso// rdo rje dges pa'i dbyingasu gyur nas/ phyag tu gan so// de nas rdo rje dges mI'i dbyings las
10a6(rgyud): 'jig rten gyi khams kyis cad kyi rdul na du za mo dang mats+tsha midi bzhin gshegs pa'i sku rnaMs byung nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi log so// zhes bya ba laso rdo ba dang sangs
10a7(rgyud): rje thul dang po bu rnams cas rbAs// rje seMs da po rlu bzhin/ bar rnab ra'athun pa'i la tu dzes par gyur dus kyang
10a8(rgyud): dbang chen po rang tu rgyal po'i lus su gyud te// khyim ldan 'das de bzhim ni nags pa rna par sdang lad gyi thugs la gnas nas/ ched du dA 'di cing du rjongad // e ma thams cad khyen
10b1(rgyud): kun gyi// legs phyin nang na bdag mchog pas/ rnam pa rtog bral ba ngag gi/ nges par debs pa skyed pa yin/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' rab tu dga' ba'i rgyal po'i sku de/ 
10b2(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs ka nas byung ste// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rgyab na// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas yang ka nod cing bzhugs par gyu ro// de nas bcom ldan
10b3(rgyud): 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyes par byed pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rabar tu dgas pa bla na me/ 
10b4(rgyud): ba'i ye shes kyi dam tshig sos can gi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa'i seMs can mgu bar bya ba dang // thams cad bde ba dang // yid bde ba myong bar bya ba nas// de na bzhin gshegs
10b5(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi dbes pa'i bla na med pa dang pa grub bzod pa nga'i bar du zas bu de dag gi phyir rdo rje dgas pa de bya chub sems dpa' chen po rab tu dpa' ba'i rgyal po de'i lagu tu de bzhi du
10b6(rgyud): byin// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rdo rje dges pa zhes rdo rje zhes bya ba'i dbang gis dbang skur// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje dgyes pa'i dbyings de bzhin bshes
10b7(rgyud): pa thams cad byeg so zhes bya bas rab tu dges par byed brji ched du rjod pa 'di cing du rjod do// sangs rgyas kun gyi legs sbyid pa// 'di ni rab tu 'jug byed pas// rdo rje thams cad rjenas
10b8(rgyud): ba ra byed// lha rdzas dge ba spel ba'i// byang chub kyi sems dpa' chen po dang // de bzhin gshegs pa rnams spyan dring ba'i dam tshig dang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyes par byed pa'i ye shes dang / 
11a1(rgyud): dgas pa chen po dang 'di bani ni// de bzhing gshems pa rnams kyi dmachod chen pos sems pa'o// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems pa' chen po// nam kha'i snying po'i da
11a2(rgyud): byub/ rin po 'i byi gyis rnas di 'i nas na pa'i de na la ljongs pa na // de dan pa na thathams pa kyi ming seM kyis byung 'di bzhi gnems pa rnams pa kyi nga rdzog
11a3(rgyud): grags gnas drung // 'adz+ra rang na/ de sa de 'a sa shenasu pa rnams kyi thams kanas rgyu mthun pa ljin/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge la ni thams cad nam dma'a' dang rnam pa'id kyi
11a4(rgyud): shes shin du rtogs pa yin pa'i phyir// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa de nyid de/ namakha' thams cad kyi 'di zer du gyur nas byung ngo // nam mkha' thams cad kyi 'od zer de dag gis 'jig rten
11a5(rgyud): kyi khams thams cad snang bar byas nas/ thams sad pa dkyis zur byur to// de nasu de bzhin gshegs pa/ dAm sa kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis rnam pa'i dkyis sbyi ng+ge zer de dag
11a6(rgyud): 'a byang chu kyi nga ra nga bu dru dag ro// de sa rin pa 'i mid kyis de yin/ 'dzin kyi khams pas ca
11a7(rgyud): rdul pa d+ha phra mo dang mnyam parjid badzin 'dis gshenas pa rnams kyi cur zur nas// de bzhi gshegs thams cad med ngapa la grogs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad rdu 'phrul
11b1(rgyud): dang / cho 'phrul rnams 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du snang bar byas nas// rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni// nam mkha'i khams thams cad kyi snying po las shin du byung ba dang / 
11b2(rgyud): rab tu rten pa'i phyir gcig tu 'dres par gyur to// byang chub sems dpa' chen po nam mkha'i snying po'i skur gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang 'dzad kyi thugs la gnas nas
11b3(rgyud): ched du rjod pa 'di ched du rjod do// kye mgo chags med rgyal ba yang // khams sum dbang por dgongs pa ni// rdo rje rin chen dam pa'i/ dbang gi mchod ni bdag yin no/ 
11b4(rgyud): de nas byang chub sems dpa' nam mkha'i snying po'i lus de bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs kha nas byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi spyan sngar zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas/ 
11b5(rgyud): yang bka' nod cing bzhugs par gyur to// de nasabacom ldan 'das kyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi nor bu rin chen rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par
11b6(rgyud): bzhugs nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dgongs pa yongasu rdzogs par bya ba'i dam tshig sems can gyi khams thams cad ma lus pa lus pa med pa'i don thams cad yongs
11b7(rgyud): 'grub par bya ba dang / thams cad kyis bde pa dang / yid bde la 'ong bar byas nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi don dam pa phun sum tshogs pas 'grub pa thob par byas
11b8(rgyud): ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po nam mkha'i snying po rdo rje rin po chen li 'khor lo skor bar rdo rje rin po che'i myu gu'i dbang gis dbang skur nas// lag na tu rdo rje'i nor bu de byin no// 
12a1(rgyud): de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams kyis rdo rje'i snying ba zhes bya ba'i dbang gis dang dur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen pos rdo rje nor pa de rang gi dbang skur ban su 'jug tsa
12a2(rgyud): cher du rjong pa 'di cid du rjod do// sangs rgyas kun gyi sems dpa' dbyin// dbang gyur de ni bdag yin no// bdug kI lab tu phyin bsan// rin chen la ni rin rkyen gnan/ 
12a3(rgyud): de nas sang sam na las kyis byang chub sems pa rkyen spyo dpa rje na po zhes kyi 'dzu pa byung/ rin po'i gyis nA ri'i rje rje zhes bya ba'i ding nge 'dzid pa sgoms par 'ams
12a4(rgyud): nas// de badzin gshegs pa thams cad kyi stod zed gyi dam tshig ces zu de de bzhin gshegs pa thams cud snying po di rang gi thugs sa nas byung ngo // badz+ra dzA dzA/ den/ 
12a5(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs lasngo byung ma zag pa 'di ni/ bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje de nyid de/ nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor chen por gyur nas bcom ldan 'a
12a6(rgyud): rnam par snang 'ad kyi thug su 'grus te/ gcig tu dres par gyur nas/ rdo rje me ma'i dngas gyur te/ som ldan 'das kyi dag gA m+b+ha nas// de nas rdo rje ni mi
12a7(rgyud): 'byed pa la sogs pa dang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdzu 'dzul dang / cho 'phrul nas byas nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni/ shin tu ga'i rjing che ba dang / rab tu nam
12b1(rgyud): pa'i phyir// gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas// byang chub sems dpa' chen po gzi rdzing chen dri'i skur gyur nas// bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs la gnas te/ 
12b2(rgyud): ched du rjod pa 'di ched du rjod do// kye ma skyes khams kun tu// snang byed gzi rdzing dbye med 'dag/ gang phyir sangs rgyas dag pade// dzin pa rnaMs kyang sbyor bar byed// de nas rtswa
12b3(rgyud): chub sems dpa' chen po dri ma med pa'i gzi rjed de'i lus// bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs las byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi g.yas phyogs kyi zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas/ 
12b4(rgyud): te// bka' nod cing bzhugs par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi byin gyis rlabs// rdo rje zhes
12b5(rgyud): bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams kyi 'od zer gyi dam tshigasems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa rnaMs kyi gzhi
12b6(rgyud): ni 'tshungs pa med pa da / thams cad kyis byede ba dang yid bde la myong bar byas nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rang gi 'od tho sri 'gyu pad+ma n+d+ha ba'i phyi
12b7(rgyud): rdo rje nyi ma'i de byang chub sems dpa' chen po gzi rdzing chen po de'i lag tu de bzhin du byin no// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i 'od rdo rje'i 'od ces rje'i zhes bya ba
12b8(rgyud): dbang gis dbang skur ro// de nas byang chub sems skyes dpa' chen po rdo rje'i nyi ma des has/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la snang bar byed cing // cheng du rjod pa 'di ched du rjod do/ 
13a1(rgyud): sangs rgyas kun gyi snang ba 'di// mi shes mun nag 'joms byed pa// shin du phra rdul ci snyed pa'i// nyi ma'i 'od pas shin du ldog/ de bzhinas yang bcom
13a2(rgyud): ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' chen po rin po che'i dpal gis dam tshig 'byung ba rin po che'i byin gyis rlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs// de
13a3(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dgongs pa so su rdzogs par byed pa'i dam tshig ces bya ba dang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po 'di rang gi thugs kanas cung
13a4(rgyud): badz+ra ke tu// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs las byung ma zag pa 'di nibacom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa de nyid dergyal mtshan
13a5(rgyud): kha dog dang / gzugs dang rgyan dang dbyibs sna tshogs par gyur te byung nas// bcom ldan 'das rnam par sngang 'dzad kyi thug su zhugs te// gcig tu 'dres
13a6(rgyud): mamathar nas/ rdzam mtshan gyi dkying su gyud te/ phyag bas cu ga so// de nas de rje rdul man gyi dkyis de las 'dis rten gi/ mas thams cad kyi ma d+haH
13a7(rgyud): dang mnyam pa'i dri bzhin gshegs pa'i spyan mas rgyung nas// de duzhin gshes rnams cad kyi rin po 'i'i rtsal mtshan skyes pa la nag su sangs rgyas 'ams cang tu tshul dang/ 
13a8(rgyud): rnas byas nas rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni rin po che'i dang / shin du dran pa yin pa'i phyir/ gcig tu rjes par gyur nas// byang chub sems dpa' chen po rin po che dpal gi sku
13b1(rgyud): gyur nas// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rna bar snang 'dzad kyis thugs la gnas nas// ched du rjod pa 'di ched du rjod do// / kye ma'o don kun 'grub pa dang / dgongs pa
13b2(rgyud): thams cad rdzogs pa'i don rdzas thams cad rdzogs byed pa'i/ 'dra med dpal ni bad ga yin no// de nas byang chub sems dpal rin chen dpal gi sku/ bcom ldan 'das kyi
13b3(rgyud): thugs ka nas byung ste// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi g.yon phyogs kyi zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas// yang ka nod cing bzhugs par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das
13b4(rgyud): kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rgyal mtshan gyi byin gyis rlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi nor bu yid bzhin gyi/ 
13b5(rgyud): rgyal man rnyeng dri'i dam tshig sems na gyi 'das gazlas ba lus pa me la rnams kyi babs na sgra gang ba bya dang / rnams ca / de na dang spyod du
13b6(rgyud): nga'i bya la nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dod chen po dam pa zlurma b+h+yo d+ha dra'i bar du 'bras bu de dag ni phyinardo rje rgyal mtshad de byang chub sems dpang chen po rin
13b7(rgyud): de'i lag tu de bzhin du byin no// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba'i dbang gi dbang skur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' seMs dpa' chen po
13b8(rgyud): rje'i rgyal mtshan gis rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan des de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la sbyor du bcu gi nas// cheng du rjod pa 'di ched du rjod do// sangs rgyas ldan
14a1(rgyud): dgongs pa kun/ yong su rdzogs par byed pa'i// yid bzhin nor bu rgyal mtshan 'di// sbyin pa'i pha rol phyin po'i tshul// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' chen/ 
14a2(rgyud): po rtag tu mgu ba'i dbang po'i dam tshig byung ba rin po che'i byin gyis rlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin lo snyoms par zhugs nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dgas pa'i dam tshig ces bya ba// 
14a3(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po 'di rang gi thugs ka nas byung ngo // badz+ra nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs la sa rlung ma thag pa 'di ni/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin/ 
14a4(rgyud): kha de nyid de// de bzhin gshegs pa mas cad kyi 'dub par byar te byung nas bcom ldan 'das rna bar snang 'drang kyi thug su zhugyis te// gcig tu 'dres par gyur nas dri rje 'jum pa'i dbyings gyu
14a5(rgyud): tephyag gnyis gnaso// de nas rdo rje 'dzum pa'i dbyabs de las 'a garten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin du thA mo dang // mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
14a6(rgyud): du byung ba la sogs pa sangs rgyas kun rtse rdzu 'phrul dang / cho 'phrul nas byas nas/ rdo rje sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin ni rtag tu dga' zhing rab tu mgu ba'i dang po yin pa dang // shin du
14a7(rgyud): tan ra'i phyir gcin du 'dres par gyur te// byang chub sems dpa' chen po rtag tu dga' ding rab tu mgu ba'i dbang bro'i lus su gyur nas ma ldan 'das rnam par snad 'dzud sbyi zugs pa sa
14a8(rgyud): nas/ da du rjod pa'i cing du rjod do// rtag tu sa par can gnas kyis/ rgyas dang pa 'i spyor / kye ma'i bdon gi rkyen na na 'an kyi rung byung yin// des
14b1(rgyud): chub sems dpa' chen po rtag par dga' zhing rab tu mgu ba'i dbang po'i lus// bcom ldan lnga 'das kyi thugs las byung nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams kyi rgyab kyi zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas/ 
14b2(rgyud): yang bka' nod cing bzhugs par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rmang du byung ba'i byin gyis rlabs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas
14b3(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi tshad du byung ba/ bskyed pa dam tshig sems can gyi khams ma lus pa med pa'i thams cad kyi dbang po za na med pa thams cad byed pa dang / yid re 'thong bar
14b4(rgyud): bya ba nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dbang po yongasu sbyong ba'i ye shes mngon par thob pa'i bar du 'bras bu dre drug gi phyir byang chub sems dpa' chen po rtag par dga' zhing rab tu
14b5(rgyud): mgu ba'i dbang po de'i lag tu rdo rje 'dzum pa de de bzhin du byin no// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis rdo rje dga' rdo rje dga' ba zhes bya ba'i dbang gis dbang sku ro// 
14b6(rgyud): de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje dga' bas rdo rje 'dzum pa des// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dgas par byed cing // ched dro bya 'di ched du rjod do// 'di ni sangs
14b7(rgyud): rnam thams thongs kyi// chang du byung skyed ston pa po// dgas pa chen por byed pa khyen// gtsug lag lazhan gyis shes mi nus// dbang skur ba ni chen po da du gyi dkyi 'jor
14b8(rgyud): 'dom gang ba dang / sems dpa' chen po kun tu spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i don dang dgas pa chen po dang // 'di bzhi ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dbang bskur chen po'i sems dpa'o// 
15a1(rgyud): de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis// byang chub sems dpa' chen po kun tu spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i dam cig byung ba'i chos kyi byin gyis rlangs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyom
15a2(rgyud): bar zhugs nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi dam tshig ces bya ba 'di bzhon ming bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po 'di rang zugs ka nas byung ngo // badz+ra drArmA/ de nas de ni
15a3(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs las byung mthog pa 'i ni/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin rje nyid do// rdo rje sems dpa' ting nge 'dzin ni rang bzhin gyis dag pa'i chos mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes rab tu
15a4(rgyud): rtogs pa'i phyir// dam pa'i chos kyi 'od zer du gyur te byung ngo // dam pa'i chos 'od zer de dag gi 'jig rten gi khams thams cad kyi spyan snga na// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor thams cad kun tu sna
15a5(rgyud): bar byas pas/ chos kyi dbyings lta bur gyur to// chos kyi dbyings de dag/ thams cad kyang com ldan 'das rnam par snang 'dzad kyi thug su zhugs te// gcig tu 'dres par
15a6(rgyud): gyur nas// nam pa'i khams thams cad dang mnyam par 'jug pa cid tsam gyi 'ang ma chen pa'i dbying su zur te// phyag su ga po de nas rdo rje bang mo'i dbyings de las 'jig rten gyi khams pas/

15b1(rgyud): tu 'dres par gyur nas// byang chub sems dpa' chen po kun tu spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po'i skur gyur te// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs par rnam par snang 'dzad kyi thugs la gnas nas/ 
15b2(rgyud): cheng du rjod pa 'di ched du rjod do// kye ma rang 'byung gdod nus dag/ dam pa'i don ni bdag yin te// gang phyir gzings 'dra'i chos rnams las// rnam par dag pa dmigs pa 'gyur// de nas byang chu

16a1(rgyud): de'i kho na rtogs pa 'di// bdag ste bdag gi lag tu byin// chos la chos ni gnas par 'gyur// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' chen po 'jam dpal gi dam tshig rgyu/

16a3(rgyud): de bzhin shegs pa thams cad kyi snying po 'di rang gi thugs ka nas byung ngo // badz+ra tI ka/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs nas byung ma zag pa'i phyir ni bcom ldan 'das rdo rje

27a7(rgyud): nga'i rdza ni zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas// ched du rjod pa 'di ched du rjod do// kye mas rdzas dro'o// yid 'od ci ni bdag yin to// de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi dri// lus nas sun la gyi
27a8(rgyud): bar gyur// de nas pa na pa segs thams cad kyi se shes dba' pa dang / byang chub chen po'i yang lag gsags pa dang // de bzhin pashegs pa thams cad chos kun du snang ba dang // tshul/ 
27b1(rgyud): khrims dang ting nge 'dzin dang // shes rab dang rnam par grol ba dang / rnam par grol ba'i ye shes ston pa'i dri rnams ni// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bka' bzhin byed pa'o// de nas bcom
27b2(rgyud): ldan 'das rnam par snang 'dzad kyis yang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam tshig gi lcags kyu dam tshig byung // sems dpa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs nas/

27b4(rgyud): gi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin du phra mo dang mnyam pa'i de ba zhin gshegs pa'i sku rnams byung nas// yang du cig tu 'dres te byang chub sems dpa' chen po rdo rje lcags kyu zhes bya ba'i skur
27b5(rgyud): gyur nas// bcom ldan 'das kyi khang bu rtsigs pa rtse mo rdo rje dang // nor bu dang / rin po che las byas pa'i rdo rje'i sgo khang gi dang zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dam chas
27b6(rgyud): zhes spyan 'dren cing // cheng du rjod pa 'di ched du rjod do// kye ma sangs rgyas thams cad kyi/ yang dag smon 'dzi ldan pa dag// yang phyir bdag gis spyan grangs pas// dkyil 'khor kun la rten par 'gyur/

27b8(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi phyag rgya spyan 'dren pa la sogs pa 'di rang gi thugs ka nas byung ngo // badz+ra pa sha// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs las 'di byung ma thab tu// de bzhin
28a1(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam tshig 'dres pa'i phyag rgya mang por gyur nas byung ste// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa de nyid do// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam tshig 'dres pa'i phyag rgya mang po
28a2(rgyud): mdems/ sa she se 'bas mams cad kyi mu 'i du zas dang bcas pa'i/ de bzhi galegs pa'i thunams byung sa yang mthig tu zhes te/ byang chub sems dpa' do rjegags pa zhes bya ba'i
28a3(rgyud): gyur gyur nas// de bzhi bcom ldan 'das kyi khang phupa rtse mo de rje dang / nor bu dang / rin po me las byas pa'i rdo Shang gi dang na/ zla ba'i dkyil 'thidang la gnas nas/ de ba' gshegs pa lams cad spya 'dren ci
28a4(rgyud): ched du rjod pa 'di ched du rjod do// rtse ma sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// rdo rje'i zhags pa pad mo'i bdag/ rdul dran thugs pa thams cad kyang // slar yang bdag gis grang bar bya// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das

28a7(rgyud): de mas pa pas da kyi mchig spangs pa'i byag tu rang shi bya sa d+hA hU~M/ som ldan sa rang zhi ba di da do// de sa grus san gyi sa mas pa'i gyu
28a8(rgyud): mang po de dag las// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin du phra mo dang mnyam pa'i rnams byung nas/ gagacig tu 'dres te byang chub sems dpa' chen po rdo rje lhag ldog ces bya ba'i skur gyur te/ 
28b1(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das kyi khang bu rtsegs pa rtse mo rdo rje dang // nor bu dang / rin po che las byas pa'i chos kyi sgo khang gi nang na zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad 'ching zhing /

28b3(rgyud): de bden gshegs pa thams cad kyi dran 'di 'ang gi thugs ka nas byung ngo // badz+ra a k+She sha/ de nas de bzhis gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs las 'di byung ma thab tu// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi phyag

28b5(rgyud): shin du phra mo dang mnyam pa'i// de bzhin gshegs pa rnams byung ste/ gcig tu 'dres nas/ rdo rje dbang badz+ra skur gyur te// bcom ldan 'das kyi khang bu rtsebs pa'i rtse mo rdo rje dang // nor
28b6(rgyud): bu dang // rin po che las byas pa'i las kyi sgo gang gi nang na// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la gnas nas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad 'bebs shing // ched du rjod 'di pa 'di ched du rjod do// kye ma sangs
28b7(rgyud): rgyam sems cad kyi// rdo rje 'bebs pakan pa 'dag/ kun gyi bdag tu gyur pa yang // dran du yang ni gyur pa yin/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad spyan drang ba dang 'azhugs pa dang brkyang ba dang // dbang du rgya
28b8(rgyud): ba nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bka' bzhin du byed pa'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad byin gyis rlabs pa'i phyir// rdo rje se gol gi mtshan ma mdzad sa de bzhin

29a1(rgyud): 'jig rten gi khams rab 'jam rgya 'tsho'i sprin thams cad nas// 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul shin du phra mo dang mnyam pa'i// de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gi dkyil 'khor
29a2(rgyud): mang po dang bcas te 'dub nas// khang bu rtsegs pa rdo rje dang nor bu dang // rin po me las byas pa gang na pa dang / som ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad gang na par drir gshegs nas/

30a1(rgyud): byed/ 'jig rten dbang rab rdo rje spyan// phyag 'tshal rdo rje spyan khyod la// rdo rje rnon po theg pa che// rdo rje ral dri mtshon chen po// 'jam dpal rdo rje rab tu zab// phyag 'tshal rdo rje blo khyod la/ 
30a2(rgyud): de rje nu dang snying po che// rdo rje 'khor lo tshul chen po// rab skor rdo rje las byung ba/ phyag 'tshal rdo rje snying khyod la/ rdo rje gsung bya rang rig mchog rdo rje zlos bre rab grub sbyin/ mi bsung rdo rje mchog grub pa/ 
30a3(rgyud): byas 'asas rje sung byung ba/ derje sas rab rje jig la/ las kyi rje ba nu 'o// dri rje sa pa rgya myed/ skyes ma rdo rjepa mthod bya/ de rje srung ba dan pa che/ rjerje goman pa che/ na gyu

32a7(rgyud): zag tu/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad du 'grub par yang bka' ba ma lags na// ngos grub gzhan lta smos kyang ci 'tshal// de la dang por de kho nar de bzhin gshegs pa zad la phyag 'tshal lo/ 
32a8(rgyud): de ni 'di ltar rdo rje'i thal mo rkyang ste/ lus thams cad kyi phyag 'tshal zhing sngags 'di skad don/ oM sarba ta tha ga ta sU dzi pA thA nA ya/ Ang mA nan niN+ya ta yA mi/ sarba ta thA ga tA badz+ra sA
32b1(rgyud): ha~M Sha a maM/ zhes rjod do// de bzhin du 'dug ste// rdo rje thal mo zhi par nas ste// bral bas byas 'tshal 'di sngags 'di skad du/ oM sarba ta thA ga tA d+ha ra e tra~M d+hA lA Ta/ a nan mi
32b2(rgyud): ta ya mi/ sarba ta thA ga prA badz+ra rad na a b+ha Sha na tsa ma~M// zhes rjod do/ de nas de bzhin du 'dug ste// rdo rje'i thal mo spyi bor sbyar te/ khas phyag 'tshal zhing skabs 'di skad du/ oM sarba ta thA gA d+hAd+ha pra rnga pra
32b3(rgyud): brta nA ya/ ang ma nan ni n+ya ta ya mi pra sarba ta thA ga tA/ badz+ra dar ma pra ba d+hA ya ma~M/ zhes rjod do// de nas de bzhin du 'dug ste// rdo'i thal mo spyi bo nas pa ba ste/ snying kar gzhag nas spyi bas byab
32b4(rgyud): 'tshal zhing sngags 'di skad du// oM sarba ta thA ga tA pu dze kam ad ma nan ni r+yA ta ya mi ta sarba ta thA ga tAka badz+ra karma ku ru mo// zhes brjod do// de nas stod g.yogs dmar po gyon la// 'dod ras
32b5(rgyud): dmar pos g.yogs nas// sems dpa'i rdo rje ma'i bya ba rgya bcings ba la snying po 'di brjod do// sa ma sgom/ de nas grong mo gnyis kyis me tog gi phreng ba 'dzin du bcug la drang zhing snying po 'di brjod
32b6(rgyud): doka sa ma ya hU~M/ de nas bcug ma thag 'di skad du skams shig/ deng khyod kyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rig su zhugs kyis// ngas khyod la ye shes gang gis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
32b7(rgyud): du 'grub par yang mthong na// dngos zug gzhan la smos kyang mi dgos te// de lta bu'i ye shes skyed par bya yis// khyod kyis dkyil 'khor chen ma mthong ba rnams la ma smra shig/ dam tshig nyams
32b8(rgyud): bar gyur ta re// de nas rdo rje slob dpon nyid kyis// seMs dpa'i rdo rje ma'i phyag rgya kha nang stan pa dang / phyir snyan pa bcings la rdo rje slob ma'i spyi bor gzhag ste// 'di skad du brjod par bya'o// 'di ni khyod

33a7(rgyud): tu lha'i ye shes skye bar 'gyur te// ye shes des pha rol gyi sems shes par 'gyur ro// 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang // da ltar byung ba rnams kyi dgongs pa thams cad shes par 'gyur ro//

33b2(rgyud): mgu ba dang rangs par byed pa'i badre ba thams cad de la skye bar 'gyuraro// bde ba de dag kha cig gis ni ting nge 'dzin grub par 'gyur ro// kha cig gis ni gzungs/ kha ga cig gis ni re bya thams

33b5(rgyud): rdzing du ga zhu ko// pra ti ts+tsha badz+ra ho// de nas gang rjonye ba ba de 'dis 'grub bo// de nas phreng ba de blangs te/ mgo bor bcings la snying po 'di rjod do btsu goka sha shwa to me b+ha ba A~M pra ti thi naH
33b6(rgyud): mi mo swa twa ma ha ba la de bcings pas/ so sa dpa' chen po des bdag gir byas par gyur nas 'di myur du 'grub par 'gyur ro// de nas de ltar khabs bzhin du gdong g.yogs pa bkrol te// snying

34a7(rgyud): pa sems ca kyi dngos thub kyi mchog 'grub pa'i yi shes kyi bar du gang 'didi cing smras pa// de rjes gang gis gang dod pa de de sa rjod par bya rnanas don thams cad kyi ngos grug
34a8(rgyud): pa'i bya ba rgyam ye shes sgrub par byaste// ji dngas ni ga gnas pa/ rnying bar sos 'ongs par byas/ slobs rnas pa sa gnas pa'i gtong de'i mis thong bar 'gyur bar rdo rje dbyis
34b1(rgyud): pa bris nas kyang / nam kha'i ngos la snyoms par bya/ gang du ltung ba mthong ba drir/ cer yod par ni rnams par gshad/ blo ldan mi yis rdo rje'i dbyings/ lce'i steng du sboms nas ni

34b7(rgyud): yin no// badz+ra nga la badz+ra rUb badz+ra ka sh+ma badz+ra ma hAm// de nas rdo rje rigs 'dzin gyi dngos gru 'brug da'i rgyu'i ye shes slab par bya ste/ zla ba'i dbyibs shig zis nAs ni/

34b9(rgyud): rigs 'dzin len pa sbyin par byed// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor dbus ldan su nas/ las kyi rdo rje sgom nas ni rdo rje thams cad 'dzin pa las// rigs 'dzin kun tu myur ba
35a1(rgyud): 'gyur takya de dge gi snying po 'di dag yin no// badz+ra dar rang mdar rna ma dar/ barbang nga/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dngos grub dpa pa 'grub ba'i byas rgya'i ye shes smra

38a1(rgyud): rdo rje bcing ba 'dzu mo rdzas// de nas 'di rnams sgrub bshad do// rdo rje sgrub pa dam pa'o// rdo rje sos dpa'i ting ldan gyis// rang gi phyag rgya snying kAr bzhag/ de nas 'di rnams las
